md:max-w-[calc(100%_-var(--sidebar-width))]" data-pagefind-body=""><div class="hidden sm:block relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 "><nav aria-label="Breadcrumb" class="py-4 max-w-4xl md:px-4 xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]"><div class="max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="kafka-connector" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Kafka connector<a class="headerlink" href="#kafka-connector" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><p>You can set up a Kafka connector to consume data from a Kafka topic and store it in Tinybird by creating a <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/datafiles/connection-files">.connection</a> and <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/datafiles/datasource-files">.datasource</a> file. Use <code>tb datasource create --kafka</code> command for a guided the process.</p><h2 id="set-up-the-connector" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Set up the connector<a class="headerlink" href="#set-up-the-connector" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>To set up the Kafka connector, follow these steps.</p><div class="steps-container"><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">1</div><div class="content"><h3 id="create-a-kafka-connection" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Create a Kafka connection<a class="headerlink" href="#create-a-kafka-connection" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>You can create a Kafka connection in Tinybird using either the CLI or by manually creating a connection file.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><h4 id="option-1-use-the-cli-recommended" class="t-body-2 font-medium mt-8 mb-2">Option 1: Use the CLI (recommended)<a class="headerlink" href="#option-1-use-the-cli-recommended" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h4></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Run the following command to create a connection:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb connection create kafka
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>You are prompted to enter:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><ol><li>A name for your connection.</li><li>The bootstrap server</li><li>The Kafka key</li><li>The Kafka secret</li></ol></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>If you need to add <code>KAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL</code> or any of the <a href="#kafka-connection-settings">Kafka .connection settings</a>, edit the .connection file manually.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><h4 id="option-2-manually-create-a-connection-file" class="t-body-2 font-medium mt-8 mb-2">Option 2: Manually create a connection file<a class="headerlink" href="#option-2-manually-create-a-connection-file" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h4></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Create a <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/datafiles/connection-files">.connection file</a> with the required credentials stored in secrets. Check <a href="#kafka-connection-settings">Kafka .connection settings</a> for a complete list of Kafka connection settings.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Secrets are only replaced in your resources when you deploy. If you change a secret, you need to<!-- --> <!-- -->deploy for the changes to take effect.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><h4 id="authentication-methods" class="t-body-2 font-medium mt-8 mb-2">Authentication methods<a class="headerlink" href="#authentication-methods" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h4></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Tinybird supports multiple authentication methods for Kafka connections:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><h5 id="saslplain" class="t-body font-medium mb-2">SASL/PLAIN</h5></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>The most common authentication method for cloud Kafka providers like Confluent Cloud.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="kafka_sasl_plain.connection">kafka_sasl_plain.connection</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">TYPE kafka
KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS &lt;BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS:PORT&gt;
KAFKA_SECURITY_PROTOCOL SASL_SSL
KAFKA_SASL_MECHANISM PLAIN
KAFKA_KEY {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_KEY&quot;, &quot;key&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SECRET {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_SECRET&quot;, &quot;secret&quot;) }}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Set the kafka key and secret using <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-secret">tb secret</a>:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb [--cloud] secret set KAFKA_KEY &lt;KAFKA_KEY&gt;
tb [--cloud] secret set KAFKA_SECRET &lt;KAFKA_SECRET&gt;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><h5 id="saslscram-sha-256-or-scram-sha-512" class="t-body font-medium mb-2">SASL/SCRAM-SHA-256 or SCRAM-SHA-512</h5></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>For Kafka clusters using SCRAM authentication:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="kafka_sasl_scram.connection">kafka_sasl_scram.connection</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">TYPE kafka
KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS &lt;BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS:PORT&gt;
KAFKA_SECURITY_PROTOCOL SASL_SSL
KAFKA_SASL_MECHANISM SCRAM-SHA-256
KAFKA_KEY {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_KEY&quot;, &quot;key&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SECRET {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_SECRET&quot;, &quot;secret&quot;) }}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Replace <code>SCRAM-SHA-256</code> with <code>SCRAM-SHA-512</code> if your cluster uses SHA-512.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><h5 id="sasloauthbearer-aws-msk" class="t-body font-medium mb-2">SASL/OAuthBearer (AWS MSK)</h5></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>For AWS MSK clusters using IAM authentication:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="kafka_sasl_oauthbearer_aws.connection">kafka_sasl_oauthbearer_aws.connection</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">TYPE kafka
KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS &lt;BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS:PORT&gt;
KAFKA_SECURITY_PROTOCOL SASL_SSL
KAFKA_SASL_MECHANISM OAUTHBEARER
KAFKA_SASL_OAUTHBEARER_METHOD AWS
KAFKA_SASL_OAUTHBEARER_AWS_REGION &lt;AWS_REGION&gt;
KAFKA_SASL_OAUTHBEARER_AWS_ROLE_ARN {{ tb_secret(&quot;AWS_ROLE_ARN&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SASL_OAUTHBEARER_AWS_EXTERNAL_ID &lt;AWS_EXTERNAL_ID&gt;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>When using AWS method, you need to set up the required AWS IAM role with appropriate permissions. See the <a href="#aws-iam-permissions">AWS IAM permissions</a> section for details on the required access policy and trust policy configurations.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Set the AWS role ARN using <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-secret">tb secret</a>:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb [--cloud] secret set AWS_ROLE_ARN &lt;AWS_ROLE_ARN&gt;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>For detailed setup instructions for specific vendors, see:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><ul><li><a href="kafka/guides/confluent-cloud-setup">Confluent Cloud setup guide</a></li><li><a href="kafka/guides/aws-msk-setup">AWS MSK setup guide</a></li><li><a href="kafka/guides/redpanda-setup">Redpanda setup guide</a></li></ul></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><h5 id="plaintext-local-development-only" class="t-body font-medium mb-2">PLAINTEXT (local development only)</h5></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>For local development with unsecured Kafka:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="kafka_plaintext.connection">kafka_plaintext.connection</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">TYPE kafka
KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS localhost:9092
KAFKA_SECURITY_PROTOCOL PLAINTEXT
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-warning text-error"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12 1.25C6.063 1.25 1.25 6.063 1.25 12S6.063 22.75 12 22.75 22.75 17.937 22.75 12 17.937 1.25 12 1.25M2.75 12A9.25 9.25 0 0 1 12 2.75c2.284 0 4.376.828 5.99 2.2l-.02.02-13 13-.02.02A9.2 9.2 0 0 1 2.75 12m3.26 7.05A9.25 9.25 0 0 0 19.05 6.01l-.019.02-13 13z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>PLAINTEXT connections are only suitable for local development. Production Kafka clusters should use SASL_SSL.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>For more information on local development setup, see the <a href="kafka/guides/local-development">local development guide</a>.</p></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">2</div><div class="content"><h3 id="bootstrap-servers-configuration" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Bootstrap servers configuration<a class="headerlink" href="#bootstrap-servers-configuration" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>The <code>KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS</code> setting specifies one or more Kafka brokers to connect to. Use comma-separated values for multiple brokers:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS broker1:9092,broker2:9092,broker3:9092
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p><strong>Important considerations:</strong></p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><ul><li>Use the advertised listeners address, not the internal broker address</li><li>For cloud providers, use the public endpoint provided by your Kafka service</li><li>Ensure the port matches your security protocol (9092 for PLAINTEXT, 9093-9096 for SASL_SSL depending on provider)</li><li>For AWS MSK, use the bootstrap broker string from the MSK console</li></ul></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>If you encounter connection issues, see the <a href="kafka/troubleshooting#error-connection-timeout-or-broker-unreachable">troubleshooting guide</a> for bootstrap server configuration help.</p></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">3</div><div class="content"><h3 id="ssltls-certificate-configuration" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">SSL/TLS certificate configuration<a class="headerlink" href="#ssltls-certificate-configuration" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>When using <code>SASL_SSL</code> security protocol, you may need to provide a CA certificate, especially for:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><ul><li>Self-signed certificates</li><li>Private CA certificates</li><li>Aiven Kafka (Private CA port)</li></ul></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>The recommended way to provide the certificate is using secrets.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Create the multiline secret with the certificate using <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-secret#tb-secret-set">tb secret</a>. This opens an editor<!-- --> <!-- -->to introduce the value.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb [--cloud] secret set --multiline KAFKA_PROD_SSL_CA_PEM
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Use the secret in the <code>KAFKA_SSL_CA_PEM</code> setting of the connection file. Take into account this is a <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/datafiles#multiple-lines">multiline setting</a>.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="/connections/kafka_ssl_ca_pem.connection">/connections/kafka_ssl_ca_pem.connection</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">TYPE kafka
KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_PROD_SERVER&quot;, &quot;kafka:29092&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SECURITY_PROTOCOL {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_PROD_SECURITY_PROTOCOL&quot;, &quot;PLAINTEXT&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SASL_MECHANISM {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_PROD_SASL_MECHANISM&quot;, &quot;PLAIN&quot;) }}
KAFKA_KEY {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_PROD_KEY&quot;, &quot;key&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SECRET {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_PROD_SECRET&quot;, &quot;secret&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SSL_CA_PEM &gt;
  {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_PROD_SSL_CA_PEM&quot;) }}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p><strong>Certificate format requirements:</strong></p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><ul><li>Certificate must be in PEM format (starts with <code>-----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----</code>)</li><li>Include the full certificate chain if required</li><li>For Aiven Kafka, download the CA certificate from the Aiven console</li></ul></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>For troubleshooting SSL certificate issues, see the <a href="kafka/troubleshooting#error-ssltls-certificate-validation-failed">troubleshooting guide</a>.</p></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">4</div><div class="content"><h3 id="create-a-kafka-data-source" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Create a Kafka data source<a class="headerlink" href="#create-a-kafka-data-source" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Create a .datasource file using <code>tb datasource create --kafka</code> or manually.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>Define the data source schema as with any non-Kafka datasource and specify the required Kafka<!-- --> <!-- -->settings. The value of <code>KAFKA_CONNECTION_NAME</code> must match the name of the .connection file<!-- --> <!-- -->you created in the previous step.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>The default .datasource stores the whole message in a column called <code>data</code>. Then, you can use <a href="/docs/sql-reference/functions/json-functions#jsonextract-functions">JSONExtract functions</a> to access the message fields, either at query time or using materialized views.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="kafka_default.datasource">kafka_default.datasource</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SCHEMA &gt;
    `data` String `json:$`

KAFKA_CONNECTION_NAME kafka_connection # The name of the .connection file
KAFKA_TOPIC topic_name
KAFKA_GROUP_ID {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_GROUP_ID&quot;) }}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>You can always use <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/datafiles/datasource-files#jsonpath-expressions">JSONPaths</a> syntax to extract the message fields into separate columns at ingest time.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="kafka_sample.datasource">kafka_sample.datasource</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SCHEMA &gt;
   `timestamp` DateTime(3) `json:$.timestamp`,
   `session_id` String `json:$.session_id`,
   `action` LowCardinality(String) `json:$.action`,
   `version` LowCardinality(String) `json:$.version`,
   `payload` String `json:$.payload`,
   `data` String `json:$`

KAFKA_CONNECTION_NAME kafka_sample # The name of the .connection file
KAFKA_TOPIC test_topic
KAFKA_GROUP_ID {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_GROUP_ID&quot;) }}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>In addition to the columns specified in <code>SCHEMA</code>, Kafka data sources have additional columns<!-- --> <!-- -->that store metadata of the messages ingested. See <a href="#kafka-meta-columns">Kafka meta columns</a> for more<!-- --> <!-- -->information.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>For a complete list of Kafka data source settings, see <a href="#kafka-datasource-settings">Kafka .datasource settings</a>.</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-caution text-[#856100]"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.333 10.216a.666.666 0 1 0 0 1.332.666.666 0 0 0 0-1.332m7.114.98L10.08 1.862a2 2 0 0 0-3.493 0l-5.334 9.334a2 2 0 0 0 1.707 3.02h10.747a2 2 0 0 0 1.74-3.02m-1.154 1.333a.67.67 0 0 1-.586.34H2.96a.67.67 0 0 1-.587-.34.67.67 0 0 1 0-.667L7.707 2.53a.667.667 0 0 1 1.186 0l5.367 9.333a.67.67 0 0 1 .033.68zm-5.96-7.647a.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v2.667a.667.667 0 1 0 1.333 0V5.549a.667.667 0 0 0-.667-.667"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Use different consumer group values for <code>KAFKA_GROUP_ID</code> at different environments to isolate consumers and their committed offset.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>If you use <a href="https://docs.confluent.io/kafka/design/log_compaction.html#compaction-enables-deletes" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="inline-flex items-center">Kafka Tombstones</a>, Tinybird sends these <code>null</code>-payload messages to the Quarantine Data Source if your Data Source&#x27;s schema can&#x27;t accept them. You can inspect the tombstone records without affecting your main Data Source.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">5</div><div class="content"><h3 id="connectivity-check" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Connectivity check<a class="headerlink" href="#connectivity-check" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>After defining your Kafka data source and connection, test the connection and preview data:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb connection data &lt;connection_name&gt;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>This command prompts you to:</p></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><ol><li>Select a Kafka topic</li><li>Enter a consumer group ID</li><li>Returns preview data from the topic</li></ol></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><p>This validates that Tinybird can connect to your Kafka broker, authenticate, and consume messages. Remember to set any secrets used by the connection.</p></div></div></div><h2 id="compatibility" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Compatibility<a class="headerlink" href="#compatibility" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>The connector is compatible with Apache Kafka and works with any compatible implementation and vendor. The following are tried and tested:</p><ul><li>Apache Kafka</li><li>Confluent Platform and Confluent Cloud Platform</li><li>Redpanda</li><li>AWS MSK</li><li>Azure Event Hubs for Apache Kafka</li><li>Estuary</li></ul><p>For vendor-specific setup guides, see:</p><ul><li><a href="kafka/guides/confluent-cloud-setup">Confluent Cloud setup</a></li><li><a href="kafka/guides/aws-msk-setup">AWS MSK setup</a></li><li><a href="kafka/guides/redpanda-setup">Redpanda setup</a></li></ul><h2 id="schema-management-and-evolution" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Schema management and evolution<a class="headerlink" href="#schema-management-and-evolution" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Tinybird supports multiple serialization formats for Kafka messages:</p><ul><li><strong>JSON</strong> (<code>json_without_schema</code> or <code>json_with_schema</code>)</li><li><strong>Avro</strong> (requires Schema Registry)</li><li><strong>JSON Schema</strong> (requires Schema Registry)</li></ul><p>When using Schema Registry, Tinybird automatically handles schema evolution for backward-compatible changes. For detailed information on schema management, including adding fields, handling nullable types, and data type mapping, see the <a href="kafka/guides/schema-management">schema management guide</a>.</p><h3 id="message-size-limits" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Message size limits<a class="headerlink" href="#message-size-limits" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Tinybird has a default message size limit of 10 MB. Messages exceeding this limit are sent to the Quarantine Data Source. For strategies on handling large messages and troubleshooting quarantined messages, see the <a href="kafka/guides/message-size-handling">message size handling guide</a>.</p><h2 id="kafka-datasource-settings" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Kafka .datasource settings<a class="headerlink" href="#kafka-datasource-settings" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Instruction</th><th>Required</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>KAFKA_CONNECTION_NAME</code></td><td>Yes</td><td>Name of the configured Kafka connection in Tinybird. It must match the name of the<!-- --> <!-- -->connection file (without the extension).</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_TOPIC</code></td><td>Yes</td><td>Name of the Kafka topic to consume from.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_GROUP_ID</code></td><td>Yes</td><td>Consumer Group ID to use when consuming from Kafka.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_AUTO_OFFSET_RESET</code></td><td>No</td><td>Offset to use when no previous offset can be found, like when creating a new consumer. Supported values are <code>latest</code> and <code>earliest</code>. Default: <code>latest</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_STORE_HEADERS</code></td><td>No</td><td>Adds a <code>__headers Map(String, String)</code> column to the data source, and stores Kafka headers in it for later processing. Default value is <code>False</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_STORE_RAW_VALUE</code></td><td>No</td><td>Stores the raw message in its entirety in the <code>__value</code> column. Default: <code>False</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_KEY_FORMAT</code></td><td>No</td><td>Format of the message key. Valid values are <code>avro</code>, <code>json_with_schema</code>, and <code>json_without_schema</code>. Using <code>avro</code> or <code>json_with_schema</code> requires <code>KAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL</code> to be set in the connection file used by the data source.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_VALUE_FORMAT</code></td><td>No</td><td>Format of the message value. Valid values are <code>avro</code>, <code>json_with_schema</code>, and <code>json_without_schema</code>. Using <code>avro</code> or <code>json_with_schema</code> requires <code>KAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL</code> to be set in the connection file used by the data source.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h2 id="kafka-connection-settings" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Kafka .connection settings<a class="headerlink" href="#kafka-connection-settings" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Instruction</th><th>Required</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS</code></td><td>Yes</td><td>Comma-separated list of one or more Kafka brokers, including Port numbers.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_SECURITY_PROTOCOL</code></td><td>Yes</td><td>Security protocol for the connection. Accepted values are <code>PLAINTEXT</code> and <code>SASL_SSL</code>. Default value is <code>SASL_SSL</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_SASL_MECHANISM</code></td><td>No</td><td>SASL mechanism to use for authentication. Supported values are <code>PLAIN</code>, <code>SCRAM-SHA-256</code>, <code>SCRAM-SHA-512</code>, <code>OAUTHBREARER</code>. Default value is <code>PLAIN</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_KEY</code></td><td>When using SASL <code>PLAIN</code> or <code>SCRAM</code></td><td>Sometimes called Key, Client Key, or Username depending on the Kafka distribution.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_SECRET</code></td><td>When using SASL <code>PLAIN</code> or <code>SCRAM</code></td><td>Sometimes called Secret, Secret Key, or Password depending on the Kafka distribution.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_SASL_OAUTHBEARER_METHOD</code></td><td>When using SASL <code>OAUTHBEARER</code></td><td>Currently only <code>AWS</code> is supported.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_SASL_OAUTHBEARER_AWS_REGION</code></td><td>When using SASL <code>OAUTHBEARER</code></td><td>AWS MSK cluster region.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_SASL_OAUTHBEARER_AWS_ROLE_ARN</code></td><td>When using SASL <code>OAUTHBEARER</code></td><td>AWS role ARN to assume.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_SASL_OAUTHBEARER_AWS_EXTERNAL_ID</code></td><td>When using SASL <code>OAUTHBEARER</code></td><td>External ID used when assuming the role.</td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL</code></td><td>No</td><td>URL of the Kafka schema registry. Used for <code>avro</code> and <code>json_with_schema</code> deserialization of<!-- --> <!-- -->keys and values. If Basic Auth is required, include credentials in the URL format:<!-- --> <code>https://&lt;username&gt;:&lt;password&gt;@&lt;registry_host&gt;</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>KAFKA_SSL_CA_PEM</code></td><td>No</td><td>Content of the CA certificate in PEM format for SSL connections. <a href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/datafiles#multiple-lines">Multiline setting</a></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h2 id="aws-iam-permissions" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">AWS IAM permissions<a class="headerlink" href="#aws-iam-permissions" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>To grant Tinybird access to your Kafka cluster, you must create an AWS IAM role with two policies: an access policy and a trust policy.</p><h3 id="manual-configuration" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Manual configuration<a class="headerlink" href="#manual-configuration" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="w-full"><div class="bg-bg-darkest rounded-t-md overflow-hidden"><ul role="tablist" class="relative flex justify-start list-none ps-0 before:h-2 before:bg-bg-darkest before:w-full before:absolute before:-bottom-1 before:-z-[1]"><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="true" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all bg-bg-dark font-bold">AWS Access Policy</button></li><li class="m-0 w-auto"><button role="tab" aria-selected="false" class="py-3 px-4 text-caption text-white transition-all opacity-60 hover:opacity-100 hover:underline hover:font-bold">AWS Trust Policy</button></li></ul></div><div class="code-tab-content [&amp;_.snippet]:rounded-t-none"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">{
    &quot;Version&quot;: &quot;2012-10-17&quot;,
    &quot;Statement&quot;: [
        {
            &quot;Effect&quot;: &quot;Allow&quot;,
            &quot;Action&quot;: [
                &quot;kafka-cluster:Connect&quot;,
                &quot;kafka-cluster:AlterCluster&quot;,
                &quot;kafka-cluster:DescribeCluster&quot;
            ],
            &quot;Resource&quot;: &quot;arn:aws:kafka:&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_REGION&gt;:&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_ACCOUNT_ID&gt;:cluster/&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_NAME&gt;/*&quot;
        },
        {
            &quot;Effect&quot;: &quot;Allow&quot;,
            &quot;Action&quot;: [
                &quot;kafka-cluster:DescribeTopic&quot;,
                &quot;kafka-cluster:CreateTopic&quot;,
                &quot;kafka-cluster:WriteData&quot;,
                &quot;kafka-cluster:ReadData&quot;
            ],
            &quot;Resource&quot;: &quot;arn:aws:kafka:&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_REGION&gt;:&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_ACCOUNT_ID&gt;:topic/&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_NAME&gt;/*/&lt;KAFKA_TOPIC&gt;&quot;
        },
        {
            &quot;Effect&quot;: &quot;Allow&quot;,
            &quot;Action&quot;: [
                &quot;kafka-cluster:AlterGroup&quot;,
                &quot;kafka-cluster:DescribeGroup&quot;
            ],
            &quot;Resource&quot;: &quot;arn:aws:kafka:&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_REGION&gt;:&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_ACCOUNT_ID&gt;:group/&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_NAME&gt;/*/&lt;KAFKA_GROUP&gt;&quot;
        }
    ]
}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><ul><li><code>&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_REGION&gt;</code>: AWS region where the MSK cluster is located (for example, <code>us-east-1</code>).</li><li><code>&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_ACCOUNT_ID&gt;</code>: AWS account identifier of the MSK cluster.</li><li><code>&lt;MSK_CLUSTER_NAME&gt;</code>: Name of the MSK cluster (for example, <code>demo-cluster-1</code>).</li><li><code>&lt;KAFKA_TOPIC&gt;</code>: Name of the Kafka topic to give read access. Use <code>*</code> to allow all topics.</li><li><code>&lt;KAFKA_GROUP&gt;</code>: Name of the consumer group to give read access. Use <code>*</code> to allow all groups.</li><li><code>&lt;TINYBIRD_ACCOUNT_ID&gt;</code>:<ul><li>For Tinybird Cloud environments: Tinybird&#x27;s AWS account ID, which varies depending on your region and provider</li><li>For Local environments: The AWS account ID of the credentials you pass to the Docker container with <code>--use-aws-creds</code></li></ul></li><li><code>&lt;EXTERNAL_ID&gt;</code>: A unique identifier for your connection.</li></ul><h3 id="get-the-configuration-from-the-api" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Get the configuration from the API<a class="headerlink" href="#get-the-configuration-from-the-api" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Check <a href="/docs/api-reference#current-tinybird-regions">current Tinybird regions</a> to see the available regions and their corresponding API endpoints.</p><ul><li>Access Policy: <code>/v0/integrations/kafka/policies/read-access-policy</code><ul><li>Use the <code>msk_cluster_arn</code> paramter to limit the access to only one MSK cluster.</li><li>Use the <code>topics</code> parameter to limit the access to a list topics (comma separated).</li><li>Use the <code>groups</code> parameter to limit the access to a list of consumer groups (comma separated).</li></ul></li><li>Trust Policy: <code>/v0/integrations/kafka/policies/trust-policy</code><ul><li>Use the connection name in the <code>external_id_seed</code> parameter</li></ul></li></ul></div></div><h2 id="kafka-connector-in-the-local-environment" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Kafka connector in the local environment<a class="headerlink" href="#kafka-connector-in-the-local-environment" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>You can use the Kafka connector in the <a href="/docs/forward/install-tinybird/local">Tinybird Local container</a> to consume messages from a local Kafka server or a Kafka server in the cloud.</p><p>For detailed local development setup instructions, including Docker Compose examples and environment management, see the <a href="kafka/guides/local-development">local development guide</a>.</p><h3 id="local-kafka-server-with-docker-compose" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Local Kafka server with Docker Compose<a class="headerlink" href="#local-kafka-server-with-docker-compose" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>When using a local Kafka server, ensure the Tinybird Local container can access it. If you are running Kafka using Docker, Docker Compose is the best option to set up both Kafka and Tinybird Local in the same network. Here&#x27;s an example using <code>apache/kafka</code>:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">networks:
  kafka_network:
    driver: bridge

volumes:
  kafka-data:

services:

  tinybird-local:
    image: tinybirdco/tinybird-local:latest
    container_name: tinybird-local
    platform: linux/amd64
    ports:
      - &quot;7181:7181&quot;
    networks:
      - kafka_network

  kafka:
    image: apache/kafka:latest
    hostname: broker
    container_name: broker
    ports:
      - 9092:9092
    environment:
      KAFKA_BROKER_ID: 1
      KAFKA_PROCESS_ROLES: &quot;broker,controller&quot;
      KAFKA_CONTROLLER_QUORUM_VOTERS: &quot;1@broker:29093&quot;
      KAFKA_CONTROLLER_LISTENER_NAMES: &quot;CONTROLLER&quot;
      KAFKA_LISTENER_SECURITY_PROTOCOL_MAP: PLAINTEXT:PLAINTEXT,PLAINTEXT_HOST:PLAINTEXT,CONTROLLER:PLAINTEXT
      KAFKA_ADVERTISED_LISTENERS: PLAINTEXT://kafka:29092,PLAINTEXT_HOST://localhost:9092
      KAFKA_LISTENERS: PLAINTEXT://0.0.0.0:29092,PLAINTEXT_HOST://0.0.0.0:9092,CONTROLLER://0.0.0.0:29093
      KAFKA_OFFSETS_TOPIC_REPLICATION_FACTOR: 1
      KAFKA_AUTO_CREATE_TOPICS_ENABLE: &quot;true&quot;
    volumes:
      - kafka-data:/var/lib/kafka/data
    networks:
      - kafka_network
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="network-configuration" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Network configuration<a class="headerlink" href="#network-configuration" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The key points about the network configuration:</p><ol><li>The example uses a bridge network (<code>kafka_network</code>) to allow communication between containers</li><li>The Kafka service exposes ports for both internal container communication and external access</li><li>Tinybird Local connects to Kafka using the internal network address</li><li>The bootstrap servers address in your Kafka Connection should match the <code>KAFKA_ADVERTISED_LISTENERS</code> in the <code>docker-compose.yml</code> file (for example, <code>kafka:29092</code>)</li></ol><h3 id="creating-the-kafka-connection-and-data-source" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Creating the Kafka connection and data source<a class="headerlink" href="#creating-the-kafka-connection-and-data-source" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The following examples use default values in the <code>tb_secret()</code> function, which are suitable for this local setup. When deploying to Tinybird Cloud, you set these secrets in the Tinybird Cloud environment instead.</p><p>Connection file <code>/connections/kafka_conn.connection</code></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="/connections/kafka_conn.connection">/connections/kafka_conn.connection</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">TYPE kafka
KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_PROD_SERVER&quot;, &quot;kafka:29092&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SECURITY_PROTOCOL {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_PROD_SECURITY_PROTOCOL&quot;, &quot;PLAINTEXT&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SASL_MECHANISM {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_PROD_SASL_MECHANISM&quot;, &quot;PLAIN&quot;) }}
KAFKA_KEY {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_KEY&quot;, &quot;key&quot;) }}
KAFKA_SECRET {{ tb_secret(&quot;KAFKA_SECRET&quot;, &quot;secret&quot;) }}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>A Schemaless kafka data source file <code>/datasources/kafka_ds.datasource</code></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="datasources/kafka_ds.datasource">datasources/kafka_ds.datasource</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SCHEMA &gt;
    `data` String `json:$`

KAFKA_CONNECTION_NAME kafka_conn
KAFKA_TOPIC sample-topic
KAFKA_GROUP_ID my_group_id
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="usage-example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Usage example<a class="headerlink" href="#usage-example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="steps-container"><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">1</div><div class="content"><h4 id="start-the-docker-containers" class="t-body-2 font-medium mt-8 mb-2">Start the Docker containers<a class="headerlink" href="#start-the-docker-containers" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h4></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">docker compose up
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">2</div><div class="content"><h4 id="create-the" class="t-body-2 font-medium mt-8 mb-2">Create the <code>sample-topic</code><a class="headerlink" href="#create-the" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h4></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">docker exec -it broker /opt/kafka/bin/kafka-topics.sh --create --topic sample-topic --bootstrap-server localhost:9092

# Created topic sample-topic.
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">3</div><div class="content"><h4 id="deploy-the-project" class="t-body-2 font-medium mt-8 mb-2">Deploy the project<a class="headerlink" href="#deploy-the-project" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h4></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">tb deploy

# * Changes to be deployed:

# * Deployment submitted

# ✓ Deployment is ready
# » Removing old deployment
# ✓ Old deployment removed
# » Waiting for deployment to be promoted...
# ✓ Deployment #1 is live!
# A deployment with no data is useless. Learn how to ingest at https://www.tinybird.co/docs/forward/get-data-in
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="step numbered-step"><div class="circle">4</div><div class="content"><h4 id="send-data-to-the-topic-and-query-it" class="t-body-2 font-medium mt-8 mb-2">Send data to the topic and query it<a class="headerlink" href="#send-data-to-the-topic-and-query-it" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h4></div></div><div class="step "><div class="content"><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">echo &#x27;{&quot;data&quot;: &quot;test&quot;}&#x27; | docker exec -i broker /opt/kafka/bin/kafka-console-producer.sh --topic sample-topic --bootstrap-server localhost:9092

tb sql &quot;select * from kafka_ds&quot;
# Running against Tinybird Local
#   data               __value   __topic                  __partition   __offset   __timestamp           __key
